***corny.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:corny.html>corny</a> (40947)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:corny.html>corny</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:corn.html>corn</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-y</i>; <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> "<a href = vnd.unilang:hackneyed.html>hackneyed</a>" <a href = vnd.unilang:sense.html>sense</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> "<a href = vnd.unilang:corn.html>corn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:catalogue.html>catalogue</a> jokes", reputedly low-quality jokes <a href = vnd.unilang:that.html>that</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:formerly.html>formerly</a> printed <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> mail-order <a href = vnd.unilang:seed.html>seed</a> catalogues.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:corolla.html>corolla</a> (76616)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">corōlla</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:small.html>small</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:garland.html>garland</a>, chaplet <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wreath.html>wreath</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">corōna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:garland.html>garland</a>, chaplet, <a href = vnd.unilang:wreath.html>wreath</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:corolla.html>corolla</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">corollas</b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">corollae</b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">corollæ</b>)
</p>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">correction</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">correctio</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:corrigeren.html>corrigere</a></i> '<a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:correct.html>correct</a>, rectify', <a href = vnd.unilang:itself.html>itself</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> com- (intensifying <a href = vnd.unilang:prefix.html>prefix</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:form.html>form</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> con-) + <a href = vnd.unilang:regeren.html>regere</a> "<a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lead.html>lead</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:straight.html>straight</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:rule.html>rule</a>" (<a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> Proto-Indo-European <a href = vnd.unilang:base.html>base</a> *reg- "<a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:move.html>move</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:straight.html>straight</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:line.html>line</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:direct.html>direct</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:rule.html>rule</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:guide.html>guide</a>"): <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:correct.html>correct</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:-ie.html>-ie</a></i>
